NOTIFICATIONS  BY  GOVERNMENT
PUBLIC WORKS DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
[Üóê£¬í (G¬ô) â‡ 245, ªð£¶ŠðE (ŠH 2)ˆ ¶¬ø, 13 Ü‚«ì£ð˜ 2020, ¹ó†ì£C 27, ê£˜õK,

No. II(2)/PWD/686(c-1)/2020.
Whereas it appears that the appropriate Government has given Administrative Sanction that a total of 
30.88.38 hectares of land is required in Ittamozhi Village in Thisayanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public 
purpose, namely, Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar Interlinking Flood Carrier Canal Project. Environmental 
Impact Assessment Study for the irrigation project (ie)formation of Flood Carrier Canal from Kannadian Channel 
to drought prone Areas of Sattankulam and Tisayanvillai by interlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar 
Rivers in Tirunelveli and Thoothukudi Districts in Tamil Nadu has been carried out by “ M/s.WAPCOS” under 
section 3(3) of the Environmental Protection Act, 1986. The land is acquired to wit for the formation of Flood 
Carrier Canal. As the Environment Impact Assessment Study has been carried out for this irrigation project, 
Social Impact Assessment shall not apply according to the provision of sub section 2 of Section 6 of Right 
to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013. The 
Requisitioning body did not enter upon on the project area and canal was not dug for the Flood Carrier Project. 
No family was displaced due to the land acquisition. The Sub Collector, Cheranmahadevi is appointed as 
Administrator for the purpose of Rehabilitation and Resettlement. Therefore, it is notiﬁ ed that for the above said 
project in Ittamozhi Village of Thisayanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli District, land measuring an extent of 30.88.38 
hectares, the details of which are speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below, is under acquisition:
II-2 Ex. (424)

     30.88.38
This Notiﬁ cation is made under sub-section (1) of Section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and 
Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Collector and Land Acquisition Oﬃ  cer on any working day during the working hours.
The Government is pleased to authorize the requisitioning Department (i.e) Executive Engineer, Water Resrouces Department, Special Project Division, Tirunelveli 
and his staﬀ  to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work 
as provided and speciﬁ ed in Section 12 of the said Act.
Under sub-section (4) of Section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land (i.e.) sale / purchase, etc or create 
any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this Notiﬁ cation in the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette without prior approval of the Collector.
Objections to the acquisition, if any, may be ﬁ led by the person interested within 60 (Sixty ) days from the date of publication of this Notiﬁ cation in the 
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette as provided under section 15 of the said Act before the Collector.
  
K. MANIVASAN,
  
Principal Secretary to Government.

FORM IV
(See rule 13(1))
PRELIMINARY NOTIFICATION
No. II(2)/PWD/686(c-2)/2020.
Whereas it appears that the appropriate Government has given Administrative Sanction that a total of 7.06.60 hectares of land is required in Thisayanvilai / 
Appuvilai Villages in Thisayanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely,  Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar Interlinking Flood Carrier Canal Project. 
Environmental Impact Assessment Study for the irrigation  project (ie)formation of Flood Carrier Canal from Kannadian Channel to drought  prone Areas of Sattankulam 
and Tisayanvillai by interlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar Rivers in Tirunelveli  and Thoothukudi Districts in Tamilnadu has been carried out by " 
M/s.WAPCOS" under section 3(3) of the Environmental Protection Act 1986. The land is acquired to wit for the formation of Flood Carrier Canal.  As the   Environment 
Impact Assessment Study has been carried out for this irrigation project, Social Impact Assessment shall not apply according to the provision of sub section 2 of 
section 6 of Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 2013.  The Requisitioning body  did  not enter upon 
on the project area  and canal was not dug for the Flood Carrier Project.  No family was displaced due to the land acquisition. The Sub Collector, Cheranmahadevi 
is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of Rehabilitation and Resettlement. Therefore, it is notiﬁ ed that for the above said project in  Thisayanvilai / Appuvilai 
Villages of Thisayanvilai Taluk  in  Tirunelveli District, land measuring an extent of 7.06.60 hectares, the   details of which  are speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below, is 
under acquisition:

7.06.60
This Notiﬁ cation is made under sub-section (1) of section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and 
Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Collector and Land Acquisition Oﬃ  cer on any working day during the working hours.
The Government is pleased to authorize the requisitioning Department (i.e) Executive Engineer, Water Resrouces Department,Special Project Division, Tirunelveli 
and his staﬀ  to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work 
as provided and speciﬁ ed in section 12 of the said Act.
Under sub-section (4) of Section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land (i.e.) sale / purchase, etc or create 
any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this Notiﬁ cation in  the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette without prior approval of the Collector.
Objections to the acquisition, if any, may be ﬁ led by the person interested within 60 (Sixty ) days from the date of publication of this Notiﬁ cation in the 
Tamil Nadu Government  Gazette as provided under section 15 of the said Act before the Collector.

FORM IV
(See rule 13(1))
PRELIMINARY NOTIFICATION
No. II(2)/PWD/686(c-3)/2020.
Whereas it appears that the appropriate Government has given Administrative Sanction that a total of 23.59.95 hectares of land is required in Kadankulam 
Thirumalapuram Village in Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely,  Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar Interlinking Flood Carrier Canal 
Project. Environmental Impact Assessment Study for the irrigation  project (ie)formation of Flood Carrier Canal from Kannadian Channei to drought  prone Areas 
of Sattankulam and Tisayanvillai by interlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar Rivers in Tirunelveli  and Thoothukudi Districts in Tamil Nadu has been 
carried out by " M/s.WAPCOS" under section 3(3) of the Environmental Protection Act 1986. The land is acquired to wit for the formation of Flood Carrier Canal.  As 
the   Environment Impact Assessment Study has been carried out for this irrigation project, Social Impact Assessment shall not apply according to the provision of 
sub section 2 of Section 6 of Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 2013.  The Requisitioning body 
has entered  upon  the project area on 23.2.2019,25.2.2019,28.2.2019 and 13.2.2019 and canal was dug for the  Project.  No family was displaced due to the land 
acquisition. The Sub Collector, Cheranmahadevi is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of Rehabilitation and Resettlement. Therefore, it is notiﬁ ed that for the 
above said project in  Kadankulam Thirumalapuram Village of Nanguneri Taluk  in  Tirunelveli District, land measuring an extent of 23.59.95 hectares, the  details of 
which  are speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below, is under acquisition: 
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ

This Notiﬁ cation is made under sub-section (1) of Section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and 
Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern. 
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oﬃ  ce of the Collector and Land Acquisition Oﬃ  cer on any working day during the working hours. 
The Government is pleased to authorize the requisitioning Department (i.e) Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, Special Project Division, Nanguneri 
and his staﬀ  to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work 
as provided and speciﬁ ed in Section 12 of the said Act.
Under sub-section (4) of Section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land (i.e.) sale / purchase, etc or create 
any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this Notiﬁ cation in  the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette without prior approval of the Collector.
Objections to the acquisition, if any, may be ﬁ led by the person interested within 60 (Sixty ) days from the date of publication of this Notiﬁ cation in the 
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette as provided under Section 15 of the said Act before the Collector.
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
K. MANIVASAN,
 
 
 
 
Principal Secretary to Government.
